We are reaching out to you to request a most valuable gift that you can give the gift of life. Our organization is hosting a *Blood Donation Camp* that aims at replenishing our Royapettah Govt Hospital’s blood bank, and we're humbly inviting you to be a part of this on the occasion of our *MD Mam’s Birthday* (15th September).
  
The Blood Donation Camp is scheduled to be held on *16th Sep 2024*, from *9 AM to 1 PM* at our *Corporate Office*. All necessary precautions will be taken for donors' health and safety, and we will be closely monitoring all activities under the guidance of expert healthcare professionals.

*Blood Donation Eligibility Requirements*

• *Age*: You must be between 18 and 65 years old. 
• *Weight*: You must weigh at least 50 kg. 
• *Health*: You must be in good health and not have a cold, flu, sore throat, cold sore, stomach bug, or any other infection. 
• *Hemoglobin level*: You must meet the minimum hemoglobin level for blood donation. 
• *Medications*: You should inform the blood donation center of all prescription and over-the-counter medications you're taking. 
• *Time between donations*: The minimum time advised between two donations is 3 months. 
• *Other conditions*: You should not donate blood if you have epilepsy, asthma on steroids, bleeding disorders, thalassemia, sickle cell anemia, or polycythemia vera.
